Customs Clerk Embezzlement Case Indicted

Completed after Two Months of Investigation

The Entire Process of Investigation Has Just Begun

Shi Cunqiao, a customs clerk at the Jianghai Customs, and others, along with Su Kunnian and 999 others who established the "Slick Reporting Customs Brokerage Co.," colluded with customs brokers from various foreign firms to forge customs declarations when reporting taxes, embezzling huge sums of customs duties, totaling hundreds of thousands. These funds were distributed among multiple parties. Due to continuous losses, the Customs Office instructed the water police to investigate. After a lengthy investigation by Western Detective Pang Shi, Deputy Detective Shu Bo, Chinese Detectives Cheng Shaonian and Wang Haiquan, this major case was uncovered. Su Kunnian, Shi Cunqiao, and six others were arrested. As a result of the interrogations, Su Kunnian, Shi Cunqiao, and others confessed to their past actions and were handed over to the local court. Subsequently, the prosecutor's office conducted a detailed investigation over two months, issued arrest warrants for the remaining accomplices. The investigation procedures have only now been completed. The prosecution has cited charges including document forgery and embezzlement, requesting severe penalties. The indictments were delivered separately on the 11th of this month.

Bomb Found at Swimming Pool Explodes, Injuring People

Westerners Discussed the European War Upon Seeing the Bomb

Unexpected Carelessness Led to the Bombing Incident

Yesterday morning, at approximately 9:30 AM, a Western manager named Dian of the open-air swimming pool at 25 Jiangwan Road, together with lifeguard Wu Wenhao, age 22, from Hangzhou, were inspecting the perimeter of the pool when they suddenly found a bomb, about the size of a bowl. The Westerner picked up the bomb and stood talking with Wu about the situation of the European War. Unexpectedly and carelessly, the bomb fell to the ground with a loud explosion. Wu's chest was injured in the explosion, and he collapsed to the ground. The Westerner suffered injuries to his arms, chest, feet, and other areas, sustaining more serious wounds. Colleagues transported the Westerner to Gongji Hospital, and Wu was transferred to Tongren Hospital for treatment.

Resolution on the Property Rights of the Jing'an Temple

Confirming the Temple as a Public Monastery

Buddhist Association Calls for Representative Elections

Contracts and Judgments to be Revoked

Special Dispatch from Heping News Agency: The Jing'an Temple in this city is one of the public monasteries. The Shanghai County Chronicles and various Buddhist scriptures all record this. During the Red Turban Rebellion, monks scattered, and the temple was transformed into a tonsure lineage temple. After the founding of the Republic, the two factions disputed the position of abbot, filing lawsuits against each other. Subsequently, disputes arose over jurisdiction and property rights, initially involving jurisdictional disputes between the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Shanghai Municipal Government, then transferred to the Provisional Court. After legal proceedings, the issues further involved mortgages and disputes with the British firm Cowen. For over a decade, no appropriate resolution was reached. After Interior Minister Huang Shaoxiong took office, in order to seek a thorough solution, he, along with the Ministers of Finance and Foreign Affairs, dispatched senior officials to conduct on-site investigations. They determined that the temple was a public monastery and that the temple property could not be disposed of or altered without authorization. All contracts signed with foreign merchants were to be revoked. This was submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. The decades-long dispute over the temple property and the abbot's position finally reached a resolution. Details obtained from various sources are recorded below.

Factional Disputes

According to investigations by officials and the Buddhist Association, the Jing'an Temple was built during the reign of Emperor Da of Wu, and throughout the Tang and Song dynasties, it was a renowned scenic spot in Shanghai. Historical records indicate that it was always a public monastery. During the Taiping Rebellion, most of the monks fled, and the temple was changed from a public monastery to a tonsure lineage temple (i.e., a family lineage). In 1915, after the death of Abbot Zheng Sheng, his disciples Xue Gen and Liu Gen were accused by Lin Zhi Zhou, Yao Zhi Ting, and others before the Shanghai County Government and the former Mixed Court for violating monastic rules. The County Government agreed to the Buddhist Association President Monk Chang Gui and local monks establishing a supervisory committee to protect the temple's property. However, the disputes continued. In the winter of 1922, representatives from various local communities organized a monastic affairs conference, formally deciding that the temple should remain a public monastery. Monk Xin Ru (i.e., Gu Yun) was selected as the abbot, and Monk Yang Xi was appointed as the general representative of various mountains to supervise the abbot. This was submitted to the Mixed Court for judgment, and the temple's property documents were placed in the custody of the Mixed Court's prosecutor's office, permanently prohibiting their mortgage or sale. The abbot was recognized as having management rights but not ownership rights. Subsequently, Yao Wen Zuo of the Shanghai Buddhist Association and Hui Ji, the abbot of Qinglong Temple, argued that the Mixed Court's judgment of Monk Xin Ru inheriting the abbotship violated custom and that the嫡系僧志汶嫡系僧 Zhiwen should inherit the abbotship. They claimed that this was an administrative decision and not within the purview of the Mixed Court. As a result, they filed complaints with the provincial and central governments for several years. The former Jiangsu Provincial Governor instructed the former Shanghai Circuit Office to investigate and reply, stating that the former Mixed Court's judgment that it was a public monastery was still appropriate and should be maintained. After the National Revolutionary Army stabilized Jiangsu, representatives from various mountains publicly nominated Monk Ji Shan in May 1927, which was approved by the Shanghai Political Sub-Committee for registration.

Donation of 100,000

After his failure, the tonsure lineage monk Zhiwen secretly applied to the Shanghai Provisional Court for a preliminary injunction. He led monks, lay followers, and police, armed, to take over as abbot. Fearing that the public monastery faction might not accept this, he submitted a request to the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department in August, willing to donate 100,000 yuan. The Civil Affairs Department then confirmed that the monk had inherited the abbotship, deeming it in accordance with the amended regulations for managing temples. It determined that temples in the concessions were not the same as civil or criminal cases and were not subject to interference. The temple's property should be registered with the local government. He was praised for understanding the big picture, and the reply was gently worded. A notice was sent to the Provincial Government, and a copy was sent to the Judiciary Department and the Shanghai Municipal Government for their information. Subsequently, a letter was sent to the Shanghai Provisional Court, requesting the return of the documents of preliminary attachment submitted by the former Abbot Xin Ru.

Sale to British Merchants

At the same time, the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department appointed Xiang Kangyuan to go to Shanghai to retrieve these documents and sign three contracts with the British merchant Cowen. Xiang Kangyuan, Guo Yu Ruo, Zhiwen, and Yang Xi sealed them and used the name Chang Guan Ru. Through the Tongyi Trust Company, they agreed to sell 54 mu of land for a price of 180,000 yuan, which was later increased to 400,000 yuan. The property deeds were transferred for handover. The Municipal Government believed that the monk had deceived the government officials and secretly sold the temple property at a reduced price. It sent urgent telegrams to the Civil Affairs Department to stop the sale, but to no avail. The Jiangsu Provincial Government, based on a resolution of the political affairs meeting, instructed the Civil Affairs Department to handle the matter and reported it to the National Government for record. Subsequently, Commissioner Kong Qingzhang was appointed to join Xiang Kangyuan in inventorying the temple property and securing donations. Various parties then rose up in opposition. The Municipal Government also telegraphed the Military Affairs Commission, strongly advocating for a thorough investigation. The Military Affairs Commission dispatched Hu Renqing to Shanghai to assist in the handling. However, the Municipal Government insisted on establishing a committee for inventorying the temple property and reporting to the National Government for review. Subsequently, the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department submitted a proposal to the Provincial Government for reconsideration. The Provincial Government decided that the Shanghai Concession was still within the administrative system of the Provincial Government and that it was not necessary to establish another committee for handling the matter. It also reported to the National Government that the Municipal Government's establishment of another committee was insincere. Finally, in January 1928, the National Government meeting resolved to transfer the matter to the Ministry of Finance for handling. This would both provide military funding and resolve the disputes between the province and the municipality.

Ministry of Finance Measures

The Ministry of Finance, since receiving the order to resolve the temple's disputes, has explored three options, which are recorded below: (1) The temple should be confirmed as a public monastery; (2) Retain real estate outside of the temple, sold in parts through mortgage sales, to allocate 100,000 yuan for military funding. The remaining funds will be used to purchase Second Five National Treasury Bonds; (3) All purchased treasury bonds should be handed over to the Provincial Government or its designated agencies as a foundation for academic and religious research. The Ministry of Finance sent a letter to the Provincial Government to consult, appointing representatives from the Provincial Government and various parties to establish a Jing'an Temple Property Disposal Committee at the Ministry of Finance's Shanghai office, but no progress was made. In April 1929, the Municipal Government again submitted a report to the Executive Yuan, stating the difficulties in handling the case. The Executive Yuan forwarded it to the Ministries of Interior and Foreign Affairs, ordering the Jiangsu Commissioner for Foreign Affairs to instruct the Bureau of Measurement and Registration of Leased Land to prevent the sale, but the disputes remained unresolved.

Resolution Pathways

Interior Minister Huang Shao-xiong, since receiving the order from the Executive Yuan, together with Foreign Minister Luo Wen-gan, after researching and investigating the long-standing disputes, decided on three measures. The original text is recorded below: (1) Regarding the issue of jurisdictional authority, the reason for the reporting of disputes by both parties is that the scope of the temple's affiliation has not been determined. Currently, according to the regulations for supervising temples, the so-called competent government agency is naturally the Shanghai Municipal Government; (2) Regarding the issue of the abbot's faction, records and documents indicate that the temple is a public monastery, which is credible. Although it temporarily changed to a tonsure private transmission system during the Taiping Rebellion, the monastery system was restored in 1922 and was reported to the former Shanghai Mixed Court, the Shanghai Political Sub-Committee, and the Shanghai Municipal Government. Therefore, it should be maintained, and the temple should be permanently designated as a public monastery. This designation should be inscribed on a tablet in front of the temple to ensure its longevity. All cases of Zhiwen applying to the former Shanghai Provisional Court for judgment and the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department approving嫡系僧徒嫡系僧 disciples to be abbots should be fundamentally revoked. The Shanghai Buddhist Association should promptly convene representatives from various mountains in Shanghai to publicly elect a monk of high moral character to be the abbot of the temple; (3) Regarding the issue of disposing of temple property, the use of temple property should comply with the regulations for supervising temples. Zhiwen's previous application to sell temple property and donate funds for military use was purely a matter of personal gain under the guise of public service. The Civil Affairs Department was deceived. Regardless of the content of the contract, it was ultimately an act of fraud. Moreover, its payment and transfer were conditional on the transfer of property deeds. Since the property deeds have not been transferred, the condition has not been met, and there is no legal effect. It should be revoked entirely. The temple's property and religious items should be thoroughly inventoried by the abbot elected by the Shanghai Municipal Government and registered according to regulations. In the future, they may not be disposed of or altered without authorization.

Government Approval

The Ministry of Interior, after deciding on the three measures, submitted them to the Executive Yuan for review. The following is the directive: "Regarding the former submission by this Ministry concerning the review of various cases of disputes over the property of Jing'an Temple in Shanghai, which have been referred for verification and the proposal of solutions, it was reported to the Yuan. It was referred to the Ministry of Finance for verification and reply. Now, according to the reply, this case falls within the scope of jurisdiction of the Ministry of Interior. The files that have been stored in this Ministry over the years have been sent to the Ministry of Interior for handling. Since this Ministry has proposed appropriate solutions for the issues of jurisdictional authority, the abbot's faction, and the disposal of temple property, this Ministry also agrees. Therefore, the solutions proposed by this Ministry should be approved. In addition to notifying the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and reporting to the National Government for review, this order is hereby issued to the Ministry to promptly implement it." This order indicates that after the case was submitted by the Ministry of Interior and approved by the Executive Yuan, a notice was sent to the Shanghai Municipal Government for verification and handling. The decades-long unresolved case has now been appropriately resolved.

Wounded Soldiers Riot at the Train Station

The Stationmaster Detained, Employees Beaten

At 2:30 PM yesterday, at the Xinlonghua Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, the No. 703 freight train from Shanghai to Hangzhou, with five cars attached carrying wounded soldiers from the No. 16 Rear Hospital from Beijing to Hangzhou, arrived at Xinlonghua Station. The train's engine was damaged and could not move, so it had to wait for assistance at the station. However, when the wounded soldiers saw that the train was not moving, they immediately swarmed off the train, numbering about a hundred. They rushed to the stationmaster's office, grabbed the duty stationmaster, Guan Jiayou, and forced him to depart immediately, threatening to kill him if he did not. While they were cursing, a Shanghai-Hequ district commuter train from Shangnan Station passed by. The wounded soldiers wanted to detach the commuter train's small engine and attach it to their car to drive to Hangzhou. Stationmaster Guan tried to persuade them, explaining that the small engine did not have enough coal and water and could not travel a long distance. However, the wounded soldiers ignored him, punching and kicking him and all the station's workers. At that time, the station's police chief, Xu Shibin, saw the dangerous situation and immediately led the police officers to rescue the stationmaster and other employees, using gentle words to comfort the wounded soldiers. The wounded soldiers ignored them and cursed and beat the police chief, and also stole the stationmaster's signal flag and route sign. The entire station was temporarily unable to work. Fortunately, the police chief and others secretly dispatched police officers to guard the offices, telegraphs, telephones, and other places. They continued to protect the stationmaster and others from being injured by the wounded soldiers. They also tried to negotiate with the wounded soldiers' nurse team leader, He Shifu, no matter what, not to injure the stationmaster. If they saw an engine, they would give them priority to depart. As a result, the team leader released the stationmaster. At 3:20 PM, the Beijing-Zhabei express train passed by. The wounded soldiers again forced it to leave, attaching five cars of wounded soldiers and driving away, finally resolving the matter. The station immediately telegraphed its superiors for instructions and asked them to inform the military authorities in charge to strictly prohibit such incidents. The stationmaster reported to the First Police Section, which reported to the Lianglu Police Department for instructions.

Five Thieves Apprehended in Two Inns

Handguns and Stolen Silver Dollars Recovered

The Jin Tongchun Hotel, owned by Wu Yonggen, a local Shanghai resident, at 30 Ximen Road in the French Concession, was suddenly raided by five thieves at approximately 3:00 AM the day before yesterday. Subsequently, Detective Lu Zhuqing, the chief detective of the Second Investigation Group, learned that the gang was hiding in Room 9 of the Xin Wanli Inn at 29 Lanwei'ai Road and the Xin Zhenhe Inn at 174 Xinxin Bridge Street. He immediately led Deputy Detectives Wang Rusong and Zhang Daorong, Detectives Liu Jinrong, Shen Jinshu, and Wu Jiahui, to rush to the scene to make arrests. They found the thieves dividing the stolen money. Nearly twenty silver dollars, a six-round genuine handgun, and two wooden imitation handguns were recovered and taken back to the police station. The stolen silver dollars and real and imitation handguns were submitted as evidence. Judge Li Changnian approved the request, briefly questioned the defendants, and ordered a postponement for joint trial on the 16th. The defendants were returned to custody.

The defendant prevaricated in his testimony, claiming that the pawn tickets found by the police were all for his own clothes. Three More Suspects Arrested in the Sun Yushun Kidnapping Case

Sun's Relatives Highly Suspected

Transferred to the French Concession Police Station for Handling

Sun Yushun, a 50-year-old Shaoxing native, residing at 115 Run'an Lane, Ximen Road, French Concession, formerly owned three businesses, including the Yicheng Silk Thread Shop at Xinbei Gate in Nanshi and the Xiechangxiang Department Store in front of Yimiao Temple, with assets of over 200,000 yuan. Due to business difficulties, he had previously declared bankruptcy, retaining only the Xiechangxiang store, which was still doing fairly well. Sun's wife, Wu, 46 years old, had a son and a daughter. The eldest daughter, Huixia, 19, was studying at Ai Qun School. The younger son, Qiabao, was only 6 years old, and his parents loved him very much. The Sun family was still relatively well-off, and the interior of their house was richly furnished, attracting the attention of criminals. At 11:30 AM on May 20th of this year, Qiabao was playing in front of the door when he was suddenly kidnapped by criminals and disappeared. Sun then received a letter from the kidnappers, stating that his child was safe and sound and that he could contact them by posting a note on the back door to show his sincerity. At the time, Sun was worried after his son was kidnapped. Zheng Wenxiang, a fellow villager who had moved in as a tenant on March 6th, and his two wives repeatedly consoled Sun and offered suggestions, but Sun expressed his willingness to offer a reward of 80 yuan, which had no result. He then reported the incident to the French Concession Police Station, requesting an investigation. A few days later, Sun received another letter from the kidnappers, demanding a ransom of 8,000 yuan for the release of his son. Detectives rushed to Sun's house to investigate and obtained clues. A few days ago, they, together with Chinese and Western detectives from the Old Zhabei Police Station in the Public Concession, arrested suspects Qiu Yaoshan, Li Ziqing, and Zhou Wuying from Hangzhou, as well as Chen Lou and Chen Zhou, the wives of Zheng Wenxiang, at Nos. 509 and 516 of the Far East Hotel on Xizang Road. The next day, they continued to arrest Min Xinhao (Min had previously committed a crime and been released). When Zheng Wenxiang heard the police coming to arrest him, he escaped by jumping out of a window. Only five criminals, including Qiu, were interrogated and sent to the Second Special District Court. On May 25th, Judge Li Changnian interrogated them and ordered them to be returned to custody. The details have been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that the arrested criminals confessed to the involvement of the plaintiff's relatives, Shi Wende, and others. Detectives, together with Lu Ying, the leader of the Criminal Investigation Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, instructed Li Xiaobao, the squad leader of the Second District Criminal Investigation, Detectives Liang Zhiqing, and Patrol Officers Zhou Zhicheng and Yang Xihui, to lead police to secretly go to 290 Lujiabang Road, Sanguantang, Nanshi, at midnight the day before yesterday. Shi was out. Detectives Li Xiaobao and others waited and arrested Shi Wende (59 years old), Xu Jianqing (28 years old), and Wang Jiangqing (39 years old), all natives of Shaoxing, and found a photo of the hostage, Qiabao, and notes. They were taken to the district police station. According to Shi Wende's confession to District Chief Li, he lives upstairs at 890 Beile Road, French Concession, and works as a runner at the Yongxing Coal Company. He is Sun's nephew. After Qiabao was kidnapped, Sun gave him a photo of Qiabao with a signature on the back, asking him to find him. Wu Nianjiu, Sun's brother-in-law, a Shaoxing native who runs a stove shop on Shanghai-Minhang South Zhejiang Road in Nanshi, learned of this. On July 9th, Xu Jianqing contacted Sun's family. Wang Jiangqing confessed that he is the manager of Yongxing Coal Company and that Shi had asked him to investigate. Xu Jianqing confessed that he is a salesman for Yongxing Coal Company. The other confessions were evasive. District Chief Li determined that the case involved kidnapping and was complicated. He approved the transfer of the three criminals, including Shi, to the French Concession Police Station at 3:00 PM yesterday for handling.

Three British Crew Members of the Nanchang Steamer Released After Being Kidnapped

Had Been in the Bandit's Lair for Over Five Months

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Aboard the Daming Steamer

Three crew members of the Nanchang steamer of the British firm Taikoo Dockyard, after being kidnapped by bandits in the Niuzhuang area, were finally rescued by the Japanese authorities through negotiations with the bandits after more than five months. They arrived in Shanghai yesterday aboard the Daming steamer. The details are recorded below.

Kidnapped for Five Months

The Taikoo's Nanchang steamer is an irregular temporary cargo ship operating between the north and south seas. On March 29th of this year, the ship transported goods to Niuzhuang. Three crew members, British nationals Bai Lu, Johnson, and Halev, were kidnapped by bandits. The bandits regarded the three British nationals as valuable commodities, so they treated them quite well. However, the location where they were held was constantly changed to prevent Japanese troops from suppressing them. After the three British nationals entered the bandits' lair, they mostly lived in sorghum fields and remote mountains. The Japanese authorities, at the urging of British Consul Clarke stationed in Yingkou, advanced with both suppression and redemption. Because the bandits demanded a ransom of one million, they could not immediately comply, so it took five months for them to be rescued and escape danger.

Rescue and Escape

The captain of the Japanese garrison's military police in Yingkou, Captain Koyanagi, personally entered Panshan to negotiate the ransom with the bandit leader in order to rescue the three British nationals. After many negotiations between the two sides, they could not agree because the bandits' ransom demand was too high. In mid-July, the Japanese authorities sent troops to suppress the bandits, resulting in a decisive battle. However, they still did not rescue the three. Finally, on the 5th of this month, Captain Koyanagi again entered Panshan and conducted the final negotiation with the bandit leader, agreeing to increase the ransom and also agreeing to return the captured bandits to the bandits. The bandit leader also felt the danger of being surrounded by the Japanese army, so he accepted the terms of the 5th negotiation, agreeing to send the ransom and return the 26 relatives of the captured bandits. The bandits sent the three British nationals out.

Page 12

Released in Yingkou

After Captain Koyanagi agreed on the terms with the bandits, he returned to Niuzhuang, notified the British Consul, and brought the money and 26 bandits, accompanied by a translator, to Panshan on the 7th of this month. He first sent a person to ask the bandit leader about the condition of the three British nationals. Upon receiving the reply that they were all safe, Koyanagi handed the money over to the bandit leader for collection. Then, at 3:00 PM on the 8th, the three British nationals were sent out from a sorghum field about ten miles from Panshan and taken to Niuzhuang by the Japanese, where they were handed over to the British Consul Clarke of Yingkou. The British naval authorities specially dispatched the destroyer HMS Whitestone to Yingkou for this matter. When the three British nationals traveled by train from Panshan to Niuzhuang, the captain of the ship also went to the station to escort them.

Arrived in Shanghai by Steamer

After the British Consul in Yingkou rescued the three and brought them to the consulate, they took baths, changed clothes, and requested doctors to treat them. Because the three British nationals had been trapped in the bandits' lair for a long time and it was summer, they appeared haggard. The British Consul sent a telegram to Shanghai to report the matter. The Taikoo Company reported that they would stay at the consulate for a few days and wait for the ship to return to Shanghai. The Taikoo Company's Daming steamer happened to be going to Niuzhuang to transport goods to Shanghai. The three British nationals Bai Lu, Johnson, and Halev, eager to go to Shanghai, took the Daming steamer to Shanghai from Yingkou. At 5:00 PM yesterday, the Daming steamer arrived in Shanghai. The German shipowner of Taikoo and others went to the dock to escort everyone ashore and report the situation in the bandits' lair after being kidnapped to the company. It is now learned that the contracts of two of the three will expire soon, and they plan to leave Shanghai and return to England immediately. It is said that the situation experienced by the three in the bandits' lair has been specially purchased by a certain London newspaper for exclusive publication and will be revealed one after another.

Ministry of Transportation Establishes Telecommunications Equipment Testing Institute

The Ministry of Transportation, recognizing the large number of self-made and purchased telecommunications equipment, decided that it would be difficult to determine the quality of the materials without prior testing. Ordinarily, the Ministry would send the equipment to experts in various telecommunications bureaus for testing, and then make separate decisions. However, this was scattered across various locations, making the procedures extremely inconvenient. Now, in order to centralize expertise and use the latest scientific methods for testing to ensure accuracy, the Ministry has specially established a Telecommunications Equipment Testing Institute at 17 Maigen Road and appointed Shen Fuhai, the chief engineer of submarine cables, as the director of the institute. Technical experts Yu Bingjian, Xu Liang, Shen Zuheng, and Chen Zenglin are appointed as technicians. In the future, all telephone, wireless, and wired telecommunications equipment will have a dedicated institute for testing. If private individuals or individuals use electrical equipment and entrust the institute for testing, they will surely be satisfied with the excellent results.

Weiting Mountain is located thirty li east of Suzhou. Since the Suzhou Youth Association established a rural service center in the town five years ago, various undertakings have improved. The town will hold a urban-rural friendship on September 17th (Sunday) to raise social awareness of the countryside and invigorate the spirit of farmers to improve. Invitations have been sent to celebrities from Shanghai, Nanjing, and Suzhou to participate. At that time, there will surely be a lively scene. At a time when the countryside is declining, it is possible to go and see the actual situation of farmers' activities.

The association cannot do anything. Considering that Ms. Jiang Zhu is an orphan and widow, on the grounds of justice, it can only send a letter to the factory inquiring about the cause of the accident. It will handle the matter after receiving a reply; (5) Regarding the re-election of the third session of the association, it was resolved that it would be discussed and prepared for after the new association headquarters is moved into. The meeting adjourned at approximately 7:00 PM.

Yangwu Martial Arts Association Holds National Martial Arts Performance

Held at the Lake Society on the 17th

The Yangwu National Martial Arts Association will hold a national martial arts performance at the Lake Society on Beijing Road on the 17th of this month to raise funds. The program includes performances by famous foreign strongman Charlie Nilson and others in Greek and Roman wrestling, Mr. Shi Renwang performing the harmonica, and thrilling stunts and feats of strength and magic by a children's team. London Economic Conference 147

Among them, however, is only a very small problem. However, because the United States has a proposal to use silver as a reserve, the silver group in the subcommittee, which includes silver commissioners, has as many as thirteen countries. This group elected the US representative, Mr. Pittman, as chairman. Mr. Pittman is a man of strong self-confidence and believes that he has a very thorough understanding of silver issues. He said that the fall in silver prices is actually due to the chaotic pricing in India. The only way to save it is to prevent governments from selling their silver reserves on the market and stop collecting silver taxes. There was quite a bit of debate at the time, as each party had its own difficulties. So, it was agreed outside the meeting that silver-producing governments would jointly request a portion of the Indian government's silver reserves. Our country's

Representative's Mediation 148

Made great efforts in running around. When the discussion reached the point of India selling 35 million taels per year, a sudden twist occurred because Spain also wanted to sell. Its central bank has a reserve of 100 million ounces. As a result, it was agreed to sell 5 million ounces per year. The Indian government's sales portion would be purchased by the United States at 24 million per year, and the remaining 11 million would be shared by various countries, with Mexico taking the most and Canada second. Later, fearing that countries would be unable to afford it and

Fail to fulfill the contract, after further consultation, India requested a guarantee from the United States. The United States was outwardly reluctant to agree, but the result implied that the US could provide guarantees. This is

The General Outline of the Silver Agreement 149

When the discussion reached the original proposal that the silver content of subsidiary coins should be increased to 80% and that the government should not sell melted coins on the market, the Dutch representative objected again, because they did not want to be bound in any way under the current conference situation. Later, Italy also echoed this. After further consultation, it was agreed that the silver contract would be effective for a limited period. Mr. Pittman's tough attitude actually made the atmosphere in the meeting tense. However, the United States is also a country with a large silver reserve, and other countries had to show some restraint, so they compromised with each other and reached an agreement. The agreement will be implemented on January 1 next year. The responsibility our country bears in it is the provision of Article 4, that our country shall not melt currency or reduce its fineness within four years, and

Sell off the remaining silver. This is because the gold standard method proposed by Cornwall includes the necessity of going through this procedure, and this clause is specifically to prevent it. Tax Exemption for Pawnshops in Disaster Areas 151

Allowed Exemption from Business Tax for the First Half of the 21st Year

Tax Payments Already Made Will Be Offset Against the 23rd Year

The Finance Bureau replied to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating that, in response to your Chamber's letter No. 436, which included a letter from the Pawnshop Industry Association stating that all members of the Zhabei District, including Mingxing Xiangfeng and other pawnshops, requested to be exempted from the business tax for the first half of the 21st year, similar to the city's exemption of house tax in the war zone, and to offset the tax payments already made for the 21st year against the business tax for the 23rd year, please review and reply. Upon this, the Bureau ordered the Municipal North Collection Office to investigate and reply. Subsequently, the office submitted a report stating that the case also included a letter from the pawnshop association and a joint petition from Dexiang and other pawnshops, stating that they were currently under review. It coincided with the Bureau's previous order, and the investigation revealed that during last year's Shanghai Incident, the pawnshops were all located within the war zone, and their business losses were indeed a fact. Therefore, it was proposed to exempt them from the business tax for the first half of the 21st year, similar to the city's exemption of house tax in the war zone, and to offset the tax payments already made against the business tax for the first half of the 23rd year, which was deemed reasonable. It was proposed to approve that new establishments opened after the war in the 21st year should still be taxed for the entire year, not included in the tax reduction, to ensure fairness. Furthermore, the letters from the shops also included joint names of the pawnshop industry, which should be handled uniformly according to the case, etc., and a list of business tax grades for pawnshops in Zhabei was attached. The Bureau forwarded the matter to the Municipal Government for review and approval. Now, the 7343rd instruction states, "All submitted documents are noted. Approval is granted for exemption and verification of offsetting. This order is hereby notified." Upon this, in addition to ordering the Municipal North Collection Office to verify the offsetting of half of the 80% tax already paid for the 21st year by each household listed in the table, a corresponding letter is hereby sent to your Chamber for your information, and you are requested to inform them accordingly.

National Products Weekly

National Products Forum

Industry Control 163

— Yang Mang

The development of Japan's foreign trade and the best-selling of factory products are all attributed to the industry control under the sponsorship of the Japanese government. What is most regrettable is that China's industry associations have very little power and inconsistent methods. Therefore, they still seek their own interests, only caring about individual development and lacking the spirit of cooperation to face the outside world together. Compared with the Japanese, who are willing to sacrifice and advance aggressively, and give industry associations great power, it is really incomparable. However, in practice industry control, not only does China's industrial and commercial sector currently lack this power, but in fact there are also great difficulties. In practice, the most important factors are three: First, statistics; second, talents; third, morality. Without accurate statistics, the waxing and waning of prosperity and decline are baseless. If you don't know others and you don't know yourself, it's like a rabble suddenly facing a complete army. How can you not fail? How can you not retreat? Without specialized talents, management is poor, technology is not sophisticated, costs are not cheap, and products are not good. If there is a lack of people to study and a lack of skills to assess, how can you practice it? How can you get results? Without perfect morality, there is competition and jealousy, only profit is sought, and there is infighting and

Conflicts, implementing their "you die, I live" tactics, and even arbitrarily breaking agreements. Industry rules and regulations are regarded as mere formalities. The result is still each dreaming its own dream, and undercurrents rise one after another. This kind of association is equivalent to nothing, how can it last? Therefore, the reason why the national products industry is not easy to progress today and cannot face the outside world together is because of the lack of control power of industry associations. This is the most heartbreaking and helpless thing. However, people advance and I retreat, people press and I yield. If I don't realize it, how can I survive? It is especially hoped that the industry will rise up urgently to thoroughly realize this in order to cope with these thousands of difficulties.

National Products Talk

Talking About the Raw Material Problems of National Products 164

— Bingren

Promoting national products is an effective way to resist economic aggression from the outside and support industrial development from the inside. Its significance is very profound. In recent years, the awakening of the people has indeed seen considerable results. On the one hand, national products factories have laid a relatively solid foundation, and on the other hand, they have worked harder to research and improve their products. The reputation of national products is growing and they are being warmly welcomed everywhere. Looking at the current situation, if the factories can continue to work hard, the future development is truly immeasurable. However, in today's booming national products, some people are reviewing the raw material problem of national products. Raw materials, it is the mother of the product, caring about the raw materials while caring about the national product, is indeed a deeper level of comparison; and for the sake of loving the national product, we also confirm that this problem needs to be reviewed. Originally, the manufacture of national products should completely use domestic raw materials, which is really a matter of no doubt, because the promotion of national products was originally to plug the leak, restore rights and interests, if imported raw materials are used, then how to implement the true meaning of promoting national products. But the facts may not be so, let's see below: This time, the China National Products Guidance Institute conducted a general survey of the national products industry in Shanghai, paying special attention to the raw materials used by various factories. According to the survey results, factories in various categories inevitably use some imported raw materials, but this is not because the factories are willing to use foreign goods, it is really because the domestic raw materials are too scarce! When the institute conducted the survey, it also studied this problem with the persons in charge of various factories. The factories also regretted that there were no national products available! Here are a few of the most prominent examples:

(1) Spinning industry According to the national calculation, more than 8 million dan of cotton are used every year, while the domestic cotton, even in the year of good harvest, is not as much as this number, and because of its rough quality and short fiber, factories that spin yarn above 16 counts must use foreign cotton, that is, the quality and quantity of domestic cotton are insufficient to supply the needs of various factories, and the factories, in the case of necessity, can only purchase foreign cotton in moderation.

(2) Weaving industry Both cotton weaving and knitwear mainly use yarn and dyeing pigments as raw materials. Our country's yarn factories are still in the stage of spinning coarse yarn, and finer yarns above 42 counts cannot be produced, so factories that want to use fine yarn have to rely on foreign goods. As for dyeing pigments, our country only has a natural plant, and the most advanced man-made pigments of modern times are not produced at all. In order to facilitate use and reduce costs, various factories have to purchase dyes from foreign merchants. (3) Silk weaving industry In today's silk weaving market, interwoven fabrics and man-made silk fabrics occupy a very important position, and the raw material of these two kinds of fabrics, man-made silk, is not produced in the country at all. Since the factories cannot not weave this, it is inevitable that they purchase raw materials from foreign countries.

(4) Machinery industry The manufacture of machinery and its accessories uses steel and iron as raw materials, but the country only produces pig iron from Liuhegou. Wrought iron and steel are both lacking. The Han Yeping Company's iron plant produces iron and the Han plant produces steel, and its products could have met the needs of a part of the factories, but the entire company was shut down due to years of war. Therefore, today, the raw materials of steel and iron used by various factories, except for pig iron, have to be completely supplied by imported goods. Other raw materials, such as the three acid basic raw materials of the chemical industry, the iron sheets of the hardware industry, the wood pulp of the paper industry, and the tree rubber of the rubber industry, cannot be used because domestic products cannot supply or are insufficient to supply them. It is really too many to list. In general, national products are indeed suffering from a very serious raw material shortage; because they have to engage in manufacturing, they can only borrow imported raw materials to relieve the shortage. However, because the number of domestic raw materials is surprisingly small, the import of imported raw materials is also surprisingly large! Finally, it must be solemnly stated that although the current national products contain a certain amount of imported raw material components, this is neither because the manufacturers are willing to use foreign goods, nor is it absolutely hopeless to gradually improve. Everything is a temporary transitional phenomenon, and those who love to use national products must love these national products that are moving forward more enthusiastically!

National Products Discussion

Promoting the "Unity of Knowledge and Action" of National Products 166

— Xu Rongyu

"This year is the year of national products, we must promote national products." This has been shouted for a long time, what is its effect? On the customs' statistical table, the import of foreign goods has not decreased; in the windows of major companies, samples from Osaka, Paris, London, and New York are displayed, and they are being bought and sold competitively; modern ladies, they are living advertisements for the use of foreign goods, and they will not wear or use anything other than foreign goods. Our year of national products, the results are so exceptional, it really makes foreigners laugh and angers those who care. We have also held several national products exhibitions and several national products campaigns, which are equivalent to a shot of adrenaline. It is exciting for the moment, but afterwards it is still dazed. Is it that we Chinese are so stubborn and willing to be economically dominated by others? This makes me think of the "unity of knowledge and action" advocated by the late Premier. "Knowing but not acting is equal to not knowing." "Wanting to act but not knowing turns into blind work." What's the use of this? Our promotion of national products, unexpectedly, has also committed these two problems.

(1) Knowing but not acting These people are mostly intellectuals and modern ladies. They clearly know that this is a foreign product: they also clearly know that using foreign products is harmful to the country's lifeblood. But I love fashion, I covet beauty, what does the country have to do with me? Moreover, they also have this mentality: thinking that it is good for you to use national products, and it is unlikely that my using foreign products alone will affect the country. This kind of biased and ignorant prejudice is really the country's fatal wound. Because you can use foreign goods, how can I not use foreign goods? Who has the patent to use foreign goods? If this goes on, will the country still be able to cope? Moreover, this kind of person is the representative of the times Hurry up and build the dike, Shi Ying

Those who wear what they love and use what they love, even in remote villages, will follow suit. "If the city likes high buns, then the four directions will be one foot high." The reason why national products cannot be promoted is because these people are making trouble. If we want to promote national products, we must first sanction these people.

How to sanction these people? You want to persuade him, he doesn't not understand. Or he is eloquent and speaks of how shoddy national products are; how insufficient the production rate is, but instead makes the person who persuaded him speechless. I think "a sense of shame is something everyone has." For all those who love to use foreign goods, the people of the opinion world, verbally criticize them and write about them, inspiring their conscience; and the people in society do not associate with them, to increase their shame. When dealing with this kind of "knowing and deliberately committing" people, there is really no other way to think of.

(2) Wanting to act but not knowing, all those who have a little blood and a little conscience cannot but love to buy national products. However, the market is full of foreign goods, and unless you are an expert, you really cannot distinguish between foreign and domestic goods. There are also unscrupulous merchants who only seek profits and have no national concept, changing the appearance and passing off fish eyes as pearls, deliberately passing off inferior goods as national products. This makes those who love to buy national products unable to use their strength; therefore, the money wrongly sent in secret every year is unknown. However, this kind of problem is ultimately easier than the first: it is also easier to cure.

How to cure it? (1) Set up more national products companies. Taking Shanghai alone, although there is the Municipal Chamber of Commerce's national products shopping mall; the two national products companies on Nanjing Road; the Penglai Market in Ximen, it is actually not enough. I think there must be at least one national products store on every street. It doesn't matter if the scale is smaller, as long as it is not mixed with counterfeit goods. (2) Issue national products pamphlets. For various daily national products, the various road business associations or local chambers of commerce will print a small pamphlet, with all the trademarks, origins, and functions explained in detail. This not only gives those who love to use national products a compass; and also promotes the method of publicity for the promotion of national products, which will definitely have a considerable effect. (3) Strictly ban the change of appearance by unscrupulous merchants. We have no right to prohibit unscrupulous merchants from selling inferior goods. However, we know that inferior goods are not bought, which is already enough to make him suffer. Only when he changes his brand name, that is no different from setting a trap to trap people. It is necessary to strictly ban this in law and morality. This layer still needs the assistance of the official government, and the public cannot directly sanction it.

I have said this piece of words. It is nothing more than hoping that "those who know can act," "those who act also know," so that there is a line of hope for the future of national products. However, the ancients said; "There is no sorrow greater than the death of the heart, and death of the body is secondary." Almost half of the hearts of those who know but do not act are dead, and they must have their consciences resurrected before they are willing to love and use national products. As for those who act but do not know, that is like having a cold and cough, which is not harmful to the future of national products.

Gift-Giving Dialogue 167

— Ba Ling

Wife: My mother's birthday is in a few days. What do you plan to give her?

Husband: I was thinking, this year is the year of national products. Our clothes are all national products now. For mother-in-law's birthday, we should send some national product food, right?

Wife: Are there even national product foods? Which company makes them? How much do they cost? What's the quality like?

Husband: Mooncakes, meat dumplings, etc., from Guanshengyuan are all very good national product foods, and they aren't expensive either. How about we buy a few boxes and send them over?

Wife: Okay, okay... We're wearing national product clothes to the birthday celebration, so we should bring national product food as a gift. That's more fitting.

Husband: Yes, yes.

Notes on a Visit

A Visit to the Tongcheng Textile Factory 168

— Jiang Weiqiao

Nothing is truly useless; it's all about being able to utilize it. After visiting the Tongcheng Textile Factory, I began to believe this statement was undeniably true. This factory is located at Qikenyan on the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway. It has been established for ten years and uses leftover cotton waste from ordinary yarn factories, or discarded silk or wool, to weave finished products that are remarkably beautiful. It is internally divided into bleaching and dyeing, picking cotton, recycled silk, cotton batting, cleaning cotton, mixing cotton, spinning yarn, reeling yarn, weaving, preparation, finishing, packaging, repair, and material departments. The work proceeds sequentially, and the arrangement is very organized. The picking cotton, recycled silk, cotton batting, and bleaching and dyeing departments are the initial stages of work. Cotton waste, old silk floss, and discarded wool, etc., are bleached and dyed with coloring or manually picked, or crushed by recycled silk machines, or cleaned by cotton batting machines, thus becoming high-quality raw materials, which can then be spun into yarn and woven into cloth after passing through cotton cleaning and mixing machines. The spinning and weaving departments are the main workshops of the factory, with fourteen coarse and fine spinning machines and two military blanket machines. There is a grading room to test the weight, thickness, and tensile strength of the yarn. There are fifty-two looms, with jacquard heads and automatic shuttle boxes, which are extremely modern. In addition, machines in departments such as preparation, bleaching and dyeing, and finishing are also excellent. The factory's equipment, from the building to the machines, is scientific in every way. The factory building is constructed with reinforced concrete, and the roof is sawtooth-shaped, providing ample light and suitable temperature. The technical management is especially precise. The factory has a well-equipped research laboratory where various raw materials and samples are stored and displayed as research materials. Management is able to use scientific methods to achieve twice the result with half the effort. Inside and outside the factory, tung trees and cypress trees are planted everywhere, creating a dense, green shade. Stepping into it, one almost forgets it is a factory. Factories that use waste materials usually have a lot of dust. This factory has white iron pipes installed on the machines, with electric fans blowing the dust into a dust tower, so its cleanliness is unmatched by other factories. I especially appreciate the exceptionally harmonious relationship between labor and management. The workers, numbering nearly a thousand, all work together with one heart, cherishing the factory. Every time I visited the various departments, I saw the supervisors wearing yellow uniforms, directing traffic, full of energy. The workers were amiable and worked diligently. They treated the factory director, Mr. Chi Zongmo, the deputy factory director, Mr. Fang Shaohe, and the head of the engineering department, Mr. Zhang Yuwen, as family members. Therefore, the operation of the factory proceeds as smoothly as an arm obeys the body and a finger obeys the arm, with its effectiveness occurring almost imperceptibly. The factory's main products include plain and patterned thick velvet cloth, plain and patterned velvet blankets, military blankets, 4-count and 6-count coarse yarn, silk floss yarn, Ziqiang woolen cloth, Autumn and Spring woolen cloth, Lianjie cloth, and medicated cotton cloth, etc., with a wide variety of products, all of excellent quality and bright colors. Its ability to turn waste materials into valuable items is truly remarkable and can compete with imported goods. Over the years, it has participated in exhibitions in various provinces and has always received the highest awards. The walls of the reception room are filled with them, which can prove its achievements. Han Yu said: "Large wood is used for rafters, small wood for purlins, thin planks for doors and windows, and small wood for pivots, hinges, and wedges, each getting its due place; to apply these to build a house is the work of a craftsman; jade slips, cinnabar, red arrows, blue sesame, cow urine, horse dung, and broken drum skin, all are collected and stored, awaiting use without waste, this is the skill of a good doctor." This factory uses cotton, wool, and silk waste to produce excellent goods, preventing the outflow of economic interests and revitalizing national products. It is like the work of a craftsman and the skill of a good doctor, enabling each item to be used appropriately. This is truly gratifying! When I came, it happened that the factory's artesian well was clogged with mud and could not produce water. The personnel in its engineering department installed a motor on the canal, pumped water into the west pond of the factory, and devised a way to filter it clean, connecting it with iron pipes. In a few days, they created running water, supplying the entire factory. From this, one can see the spirit with which they handle matters on a daily basis. I secretly think that such reasonable factories are truly rare in the country. If there were large capitalists to help it expand its scope, its future development would be immeasurable! As for the welfare of the workers, such as gardens, bathrooms, schools, hospitals, libraries, and club facilities, I have written another article to record them, so I will not elaborate here.

Jiangsu Province's Recent Primary School Funding Statistics

4,644,970 Yuan

The Joint Office for Preparing Compulsory Education in Jiangsu Province has compiled statistics on the total amount of education funding in all counties of Jiangsu Province (the total education expenses of all counties, 11,335,626 yuan). The situation has been reported in previous newspapers. The funding for public and private elementary schools and elementary school divisions in all counties for the 21st year is listed below:

Jiangning 58,036 yuan, Jurong 66,370, Lishui 20,632, Gaochun 19,510, Jiangpu 19,663, Liuhe 46,798, Zhenjiang 109,724, Danyang 85,350, Jintan 47,511, Liyang 78,945, Yangzhong 6,762, Shanghai 57,383, Songjiang 125,023, Nanhui 131,064, Qingpu 7,900, Fengxian 31,080, Jinshan 53,743, Chuansha 40,838, Taicang 60,144, Jiading 83,058, Baoshan 53,491, Chongming 48,729, Haimen 66,081, Wuxian 346,717, Changshu 194,427, Kunshan 93,337, Wujiang 149,588, Wujin 218,815, Wuxi 362,294, Yixing 144,440, Jiangyin 150,152, Jingjiang 39,702, Nantong 212,787, Rugao 195,874, Taixing 58,462, Huaiyin 20,171, Huaian 59,745, Siyang 15,060, Lianshui 51,914, Funing 48,646, Yancheng 123,670, Jiangdu 56,964, Yizheng 25,237, Dongtai 45,091, Xinghua 60,540, Taixian 59,280, Gaoyou 22,320, Baoying 28,668, Gangshan 79,545, Fengxian 38,609, Peixian 38,951, Xiaoxian 42,165, Dangshan 20,607, Pixian 27,574, Suqian 39,408, Suining 25,024, Donghai 13,110, Guanyun 34,214, Shuyang 2,349, Ganyu 36,333, Qidong 52,640. The total for all the above is 4,644,970 yuan.

(Explanation) (1) The total amount of elementary school funding is 4,644,970 yuan. Those with more than 100,000 yuan are 13 counties, including Wuxi, Wuxian, Wujin, Nantong, Rugao, Changshu, Jiangyin, Wujiang, Yixing, Nanhui, Songjiang, Yancheng, and Zhenjiang (366,294 to 109,724 yuan). The remaining 48 counties, except for Yangzhong, which has only 6,722 yuan, all have more than 10,000 yuan, with an average of 76,147.05 yuan per county. Furthermore, comparing this year's funding with last year's, 40 counties have increased funding (the most significant increase is in Wuxi, with 76,313 yuan, followed by Wujiang with 46,953 yuan, Yixing with 28,769 yuan, Huaian with 24,929 yuan, Dongtai with 23,235 yuan, and Taicang and Gaoyou with 20,000 yuan each. Jinshan, Jurong, Danyang, Nantong, Baoying, Ganyu, and Qidong each increased by more than 10,000 yuan, ranging from 10,000 to several thousand yuan. The smallest increases were in Jiangdu, with an increase of 64 yuan, and Siyang, with 80 yuan. The remaining increases ranged from several hundred to several thousand yuan.) 21 counties have decreased funding (the largest decrease is in Wujin, with 33,459 yuan, and the smallest decrease is in Yangzhong, with 234 yuan). A total of 61 counties have increased elementary school funding this year by 222,802 yuan (last year's was 4,422,168 yuan).

(2) The total amount of education funding in all counties is 11,335,626 yuan (see yesterday's statistics). Among them, only Rugao has more than 500,000 yuan. Those with more than 400,000 yuan but less than 500,000 yuan are 4 counties: Wuxian, Changshu, Wujin, and Wuxi. Those with more than 300,000 yuan but less than 400,000 yuan are 5 counties: Nantong, Yancheng, Jiangyin, Wujiang, and Nanhui. Those with more than 200,000 yuan but less than 300,000 yuan are 12 counties: Songjiang, Kunshan, Yixing, Taixing, Xinghua, Zhenjiang, Gangshan, Jiangdu, Taicang, Gaoyou, Jiangning, and Liyang. In addition, those with less than 100,000 yuan are 13 counties: Yangshan, Yizheng, Xiaoxian, Chuansha, Huaiyin, Pixian, Suqian, Lishui, Jiangpu, Gaochun, Suining, Donghai, and Yangzhong. The remaining 26 counties are all between 100,000 and 200,000 yuan. The difference between the highest (524,184 yuan) and the lowest (33,346 yuan) is 490,788 yuan, which is roughly 15.72 times weaker.

(3) The elementary school funding accounts for only 41% of the total funding in each county on average. Only 10 counties, including Wu Town, Wuxian, Jiading, Rugao, Nantong, Yixing, Suqian, Chuansha, Xiaoxian, and Wujin, can exceed 50%. Only Wuxi and Wuxian can reach the legally mandated 70%. The smallest is Gaoyou, with only 9.7%.

Ministry of Education to Appoint Drafting Committee for Normal School Curriculum 170

Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education Sends Military Veterinary Students for Examination 171

This year, Nanjing Military Medical School and Beiping Veterinary School will simultaneously send letters to the provincial governments to recruit students during the summer vacation, according to the prescribed quota. Jiangsu is allowed to send three students for the 25th term of the medical department and general department of the Military Medical School, one student for the 18th term of the pharmacy department, and two regular students for the 17th term of the Veterinary School. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education is in charge of the above-mentioned examinations. The results of the examinations conducted on the 7th, 8th, and 9th of this month showed that there were not many applicants and their performance was not satisfactory. Apart from the veterinary school's re-examination, which is approaching, it is necessary to inquire with Beiping Veterinary School whether to continue recruitment. The Military Medical School students are scheduled to continue recruitment on the 16th and 17th of this month. Both Military Medical School and Veterinary School are under the chairmanship of the Ministry of Military Affairs. Applicants should be graduates of senior high school to be eligible for admission. After entering the school, all expenses for food, lodging, clothing, and books are covered by the school, and a monthly allowance of four yuan is provided. Furthermore, medicine is a specialized scientific talent, and there are few researchers in the field of veterinary medicine in the country, but there is a great need. It is a pity that high school graduates with aspirations for advancement who have not had the opportunity to further their studies should miss this opportunity.

Joint Conference on School Affairs Design of Jinan University and Municipal Education Bureau Experimental School 178

Passed Various Budget Plans and Regulations

In order to expand experimental education, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau is jointly operating an experimental school with National Jinan University in Zhenru this year. The main purpose is to experiment with production-based labor education. The first meeting of the school affairs design committee was held in Hua'an Building on the 8th, attended by Pan Gongzhan, Mi Jifang, Guo Yicen, Rao Zhuhua, Zheng Hongnian, Hu Shuyi, Zhang Yaoxiang, Chen Tianyu, Zhou Feicheng, Chen Bai, Zeng Chun, Dian Chen Kemei, Zhang Weiyi, and Zheng Baoning. Zhang Liyuan was present. Gu Zenghua presided over the meeting, and Zhang Weiyi took the minutes.

Reports 179

(1) Director Pan reported: A. Purpose of the meeting. B. The Municipal Education Bureau and Jinan University jointly operated the Zhenru Education Experiment Zone, but it was suspended midway due to the January 28th Incident. Now, in order to implement production education, we are jointly operating an experimental school with Jinan University again. We hope that we will focus our efforts on production education and achieve good results in the future. (2) Principal Zheng reported: A. The school has received the assistance of the Municipal Education Bureau, and the scope has been expanded. We hope that both parties will work hard to create a more perfect school in the future. B. The school building is currently rented from a company, with rent of more than 3,000 yuan per year. Moreover, the building is not suitable for use as a classroom, so a new school building must be built in the future. The construction of the school building should not be luxurious, but should be clear, practical, and suitable for the countryside. C. The school is both for the internship of teachers and students from both parties. Please ask Director Zhang to draft the internship method and then submit it to the school affairs committee for approval. (3) Director Zhang reported: A. Preparation process. B. Current situation. C. Construction of factory and farm.

Resolutions 180

(1) How should the funds for the construction of the factory and farm be raised? It was resolved that the construction funds of 1,000 yuan should be shared equally by Jinan University and the Municipal Education Bureau. (2) How should the tuition and miscellaneous fees collected this semester be distributed? It was resolved that in addition to being used for repairing houses and adding school equipment, the remainder should be used to purchase books, sports equipment, and instruments. (3) The school's expenses are shared by Jinan University and the Municipal Education Bureau. How should the reimbursement method be determined? It was resolved that the teaching salary of 818 yuan should be borne by Jinan University, and other staff salaries, wages, and public funds should be disbursed from the subsidy item of the Municipal Education Bureau. All reimbursements should first be submitted to the Finance Office of Jinan University for review and then submitted to the Municipal Education Bureau. (4) Please approve the budget book for this semester. It was resolved to approve the budget after review. (5) Please approve the school plan. It was resolved to approve the plan after revision. (6) Please approve the rules of procedure for the school affairs committee. It was resolved to approve the rules after revision. (7) Please approve the rules of procedure for the experimental design committee. It was resolved to approve the rules after revision. (8) Please approve the rules of procedure for the Department of Education and Guidance and the Department of General Affairs. It was resolved to approve the rules after revision. (9) Please approve the regulations for the appointment and service of class teachers and subject teachers. It was resolved to approve the regulations after revision. (10) How should the text of various regulations be modified if there are any inappropriate parts? It was resolved that Mr. Hu Shuyi, Chen Bai, and Zhang Liyuan should revise the text of each regulation in detail.

One of the Shenbao Series of Books 183

Publication of the Soviet Union's Second Five-Year Plan

In the fifteen years since the revolution in the Soviet Union, its economic development has gone through the revolutionary period, the recovery period, and entered the transformation period, completing the entire national economic transformation period. This fourth period, from January 1st of this year to 1937, is the period of the second five-year plan, which is characterized by the realization of a socialist society and the achievement of complete economic independence from capitalism. This plan has great significance in the history of Soviet economic construction. Ms. Fan Ying, from the standpoint of objective research, has specially compiled this book, which vividly describes the outline of the second five-year plan in order to meet the needs of studying the Soviet Union. The book has twelve chapters, rich in content, with eight beautiful illustrations. The actual price is 25 cents. It is published by the Special Distribution Department of this building. A special price will be offered for the fall semester for one month. Ten or more books are discounted by 30%.

Commercial News

Financial Swaps Approaching; Gold Market Continues to Stabilize

Silver Prices Rise; Raw Gold Cheaper; Off-Market Prices Once Plummet

Confidence Strengthens; Short Squeeze Intensifies; Rebound of Seventy Cents

The gold market fell and rebounded yesterday, and the situation was extremely firm in the first half of the day. As financial swaps approached, confidence was quite good. In the early morning, the prices of silver in Britain and the United States rose, and foreign exchange also rose. The forward price of silver in the Gold Exchange also rose by 1.3%. US cotton rose by 3 pounds, and US wheat rose by 0.625. Stocks fell by 7.5 cents. The price of raw gold in London plummeted again by 1 shilling and 2.5 pence. The gross market opened, initially calling for 17-18 yuan, but quickly rose. The short squeeze continued strongly. In addition, there was a rumor that HSBC's listing of US dollars and shillings had shrunk by 0.125, which further boosted the situation. Reuters reported that Senator Harrison, chairman of the Economic Committee of the US Senate, had urgently requested the President to implement a reasonable expansion plan to raise prices, which was a necessary policy. At this point, the market declined slightly. After entering the market, the situation fluctuated, but the trend was stable. The overseas market was like this, and the result was unexpectedly stable. The premium price was increased by 260 yuan. The market situation in the first half of the day is recorded below.

The market opened at 812.2 yuan, a small increase of 3.6 yuan from the previous close. Spot goods opened at 1 yuan. The foreign exchange market opened with the near-term selling price of British exchange at 1 shilling and 3.25 pence, and the US exchange at 29.125 yuan. Hengyu, Hengchang, Yongzhao, Fengchang, Zhengchang, Yuansheng, Yongzhi, Fengyong, and others jointly purchased strips, and gradually rose from 1 yuan, but the banks' appetite was blocked, and Dalian gangs and Fuyu and others supplied, so there was a lot of struggle. When it was learned that HSBC's listing of British and American currencies had shrunk by 0.125, Hengyu and others re-entered, and it rose to 6.5 yuan. Foreign cables were slightly unfavorable. Huabi came out with US dollars for October at 0.125, Citibank blocked US dollars for November at 3.125, and Ruixing, Hengyu, Fuchang, and others sold spot goods, forming a downward trend. Pangen also blocked US dollars for November at 3.75, and it dropped to 3.8 yuan. After this, there was a big rise and rotation. Yuanxing Yongxian bought and it was difficult to fall. The bank blocked US dollars for November at 3.75, and the situation stabilized. Later, Hengtai, Hengyu, Fushun, and others entered, and US dollars for November at 3.75 were difficult to settle, and they were pushed up to 6.8 yuan. Shanghai blocked half a yuan for December, and Ruixing, Wanxing, Fuchang, Yuanchun, and others all sold, and it fell again to 4.2 yuan. Wanxing, Yuanxing, Yong and others trended lower and then accepted, rising to 6.3 yuan. Ruikang supplied, and it fell back into 5 yuan. After some rotation, the midday close was 825.5 yuan. After the close, it rose slightly at first, and Shunli Hengxing came to sell, falling to within 5 yuan. Spot goods were auctioned at 5.5 yuan. The highest price in the first half of the day was 826.8 yuan, and the lowest price was 821 yuan, a difference of 5.8 yuan. As a result, it rose slightly by 7 cents compared to the previous close.

The revealed price was 8.5 yuan due to HSBC's listing of US dollars shrinking by 0.125. The combined standard gold price was 842 yuan. In terms of the closing price, it was pressed by about 16 yuan, more than 3 yuan weaker than the previous close. The book entry price for this month was 832 yuan, and for October it was 826 yuan. The replenishment water in the morning was 832 yuan. The spot market was quiet, and transactions were limited. The premium price in the market was increased by 260 yuan, and there was a lack of buyers, and the trend was quite sluggish. Financial swaps continued to be quiet. Shaanxi New Cotton Suffers Flood Damage

According to Shaanxi communications, Shaanxi cotton fields have suffered heavy losses due to flooding, accounting for about 20% of the total cotton field area in the province. Furthermore, due to insufficient rainfall during the dog days, many cotton bolls have fallen off. The yield per mu has decreased by one-third to one-half in several counties, greatly affecting the province's total output.
